### Round 2: Brazilian Grand Prix
*Date: 1999-04-11*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 6: Canadian Grand Prix
*Date: 1999-06-13*

#### Qualifying Results
